[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Issue Overview[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fuzzing test for the `handler_aim` fuzzer in Wireshark has identified a [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcritical buffer overflow vulnerability. The test was configured with the following [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparameters:[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Fuzzer: handler_aim[0m                                                               [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Runs: [0m[1;36m100[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Max length: [0m[1;36m1024[0m[39m bytes[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fuzzer successfully triggered a buffer overflow that was caught by the runtime [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer overflow detection mechanism [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`*** buffer overflow detected ***: [0m            [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Vulnerability Type[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis is a **buffer overflow vulnerability** in memory copy operations. The issue is[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdetected at the `memcpy` operation level through Fortify Source protections, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindicating that data is being copied beyond the bounds of the destination buffer.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Key Observations[0m                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Crash Location**: The buffer overflow occurs in the following call stack:[0m      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Triggering Context**: The vulnerability is triggered during the dissection of [0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3303[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[35m/[0m[39m*[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3304[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39m * For now, we treat bogus values as meaning[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3305[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39m * [0m[32m"ASCII"[0m[39m rather than reporting an error,[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3306[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39m * for the benefit of old dissectors written[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3307[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39m * when the last argument to [0m[1;35mproto_tree_add_item[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3308[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39m * was a bool for the byte order, not an[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3309[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39m * encoding value, and passed non-zero values[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3310[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39m * other than true to mean [0m[32m"little-endian"[0m[39m.[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3311[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39m *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3312[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39mstrptr = [0m[1;35mtvb_get_ascii_string[0m[1;39m([0m[39mscope, tvb, offset, length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3313[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39mbreak;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3314[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3315[0m[39m:   [0m[39mcase ENC_UTF_8:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3316[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39mstrptr = [0m[1;35mtvb_get_utf_8_string[0m[1;39m([0m[39mscope, tvb, offset, length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBased on the evaluation report and code snippets, I've identified a critical buffer[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moverflow vulnerability in the `aim_get_buddyname` function at [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/src/wireshark/epan/dissectors/[0m[95mpacket-aim.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;36m591[0m[39m`. The root cause analysis reveals [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmultiple interconnected bugs:[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Core Issues Identified[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Primary Buffer Overflow [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLine [0m[1;36m591[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**: [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Allocates fixed [0m[1;36m256[0m[39m-byte buffer [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m586[0m[1;39m)[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Reads [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m-byte length field from network packet [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m588[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - can be [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m65535[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Copies `buddyname_length` bytes without bounds validation[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If `buddyname_length > [0m[1;36m256[0m[39m`, buffer overflow occurs[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Incorrect Offset Calculation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLine [0m[1;36m591[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**:[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Uses `[0m[1;35mtvb_get_ptr[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb,offset,[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` which only validates [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m byte available[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Reads from `offset` instead of `offset+[0m[1;36m2[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mshould skip [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m-byte length field[0m[1;39m)[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This copies the length field bytes as part of the buddy name data[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Insufficient Buffer Bounds Verification**:[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mtvb_get_ptr[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb,offset,[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` validates only [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m byte, not `buddyname_length` [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbytes[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Can read beyond packet boundary even with bounds checking on destination[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Critical Logic to Preserve[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The function must continue to support [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m-byte length fields [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`uint16_t`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m as called[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mby `dissect_aim_chat_outgoing_msg` and `dissect_aim_chat_incoming_msg`[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Must maintain backward compatibility with existing callers[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The return value semantics [0m[1;39m([0m[39mreturning buddyname_length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m must be preserved[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Memory must be allocated using the wmem allocator pool for proper memory [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmanagement[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Evidence from Similar Code[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe codebase shows the correct pattern in multiple places:[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `dissect_aim_buddyname` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m846[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m866[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: Uses safe `[0m[1;35mtvb_format_text[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mproto_tree_add_item[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `aim_get_message` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m597[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m672[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: Validates `msg_length > [0m[1;36m999[0m[39m` before processing [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1000[0m[39m-byte buffer[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `dissect_aim_tlv` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m1324[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1380[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: Correctly reads length at offset, then [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mincrements offset by [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m before extracting data[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Approach: Rewrite `aim_get_buddyname` Using Safe Wireshark tvbuff API[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe optimal fix is to replace the unsafe manual allocation and memcpy with [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWireshark's built-in safe string extraction functions. This approach:[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Eliminates manual buffer size management[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Provides automatic bounds checking against both destination buffer and source [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtvbuff[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Handles character encoding properly[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Follows Wireshark coding standards and patterns[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Implementation Steps[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Modify `aim_get_buddyname` function [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m581[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m594[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mReplace the current implementation with:[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstatic int[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35maim_get_buddyname[0m[1;39m([0m[39mwmem_allocator_t *pool, uint8_t **name, tvbuff_t *tvb, int [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moffset[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m{[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    uint16_t buddyname_length;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Read [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m-byte length field from network packet[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    buddyname_length = [0m[1;35mtvb_get_ntohs[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Extract buddy name using safe tvb function[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m offset+[0m[1;36m2[0m[39m skips the [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m-byte length field[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m tvb_get_string_enc automatically:[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m   - Validates buddyname_length bytes are available in tvbuff[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m   - Allocates exact memory needed [0m[1;39m([0m[39mno fixed buffer size[0m[1;39m)[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m   - Throws exception if bounds exceeded [0m[1;39m([0m[39mproper error handling[0m[1;39m)[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m   - Handles UTF-[0m[1;36m8[0m[39m encoding[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpool[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        *name = [0m[1;35mtvb_get_string_enc[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpool, tvb, offset + [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m, buddyname_length, [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mENC_UTF_8|ENC_NA[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        *name = NULL;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    return buddyname_length;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Key Changes**:[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Remove manual `[0m[1;35mwmem_alloc[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpool, [0m[1;36m256[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` allocation[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Remove unsafe `memcpy` and `tvb_get_ptr` usage[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Use `[0m[1;35mtvb_get_string_enc[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` which provides:[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Automatic bounds validation against tvbuff via `[0m[1;35mensure_contiguous[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Dynamic allocation of exact size needed[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Proper exception handling if packet is malformed[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Correct offset calculation: `offset + [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m` to skip [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m-byte length field[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Preserve existing return value semantics[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Update `dissect_aim_chat_incoming_msg` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m2004[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mFix incorrect offset in proto_tree_add_string:[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Change from:[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mproto_tree_add_string[0m[1;39m([0m[39mchat_tree, hf_aim_chat_screen_name, tvb, [0m[1;36m31[0m[39m, [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuddyname_length, buddyname[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m To:[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mproto_tree_add_string[0m[1;39m([0m[39mchat_tree, hf_aim_chat_screen_name, tvb, [0m[1;36m32[0m[39m, [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuddyname_length, buddyname[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Rationale**: The buddy name data starts at offset [0m[1;36m32[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m30[0m[39m + [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m-byte length field[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnot [0m[1;36m31[0m[39m.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This Fix is Optimal[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Security**: [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `tvb_get_string_enc` validates bounds automatically via `[0m[1;35mensure_contiguous[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mat line [0m[1;36m2913[0m[39m of tvbuff.c[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Throws exceptions on malformed packets instead of crashing[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No manual buffer size limits to maintain[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Correctness**:[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Fixes offset calculation bug [0m[1;39m([0m[39moffset+[0m[1;36m2[0m[39m instead of offset[0m[1;39m)[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Extracts actual buddy name data, not including length field bytes[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Handles character encoding properly [0m[1;39m([0m[39mUTF-[0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m)[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Maintainability**:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Uses standard Wireshark API patterns [0m[1;39m([0m[39mseen in [0m[1;36m13[0m[39m+ other places in codebase[0m[1;39m)[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No magic numbers [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m256[0m[39m-byte buffer size[0m[1;39m)[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Self-documenting code with proper error handling[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Compatibility**:[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Preserves function signature[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Maintains return value semantics[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Works with existing callers in `dissect_aim_chat_outgoing_msg` and [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`dissect_aim_chat_incoming_msg`[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Supports wmem allocator pool pattern[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Performance**:[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Allocates exact memory needed, not fixed [0m[1;36m256[0m[39m bytes[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No wasted memory for short buddy names[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Efficient for long buddy names [0m[1;39m([0m[39mup to packet limits[0m[1;39m)[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Potential Side Effect**: If malformed packets with `buddyname_length` exceeding [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mavailable packet data are received, `tvb_get_string_enc` will throw a [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ReportedBoundsError` exception instead of silently truncating.[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Mitigation**: This is actually desired behavior in Wireshark:[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Exceptions are caught by the dissector framework[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Packet is marked as malformed[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Dissection continues with next packet[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- More robust than silent corruption or crashes[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Testing Considerations**:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fix should be tested with the provided fuzzer test case that triggers the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moverflow[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Should verify buddy names of various lengths [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m255[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m256[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m65535[0m[1;39m)[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Should test with malformed packets [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlength exceeds available data[0m[1;39m)[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Should verify existing legitimate AIM traffic still dissects correctly[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Alternative Approaches Considered and Rejected[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Alternative [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Manual bounds checking with [0m[1;36m255[0m[39m-byte limit**[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Rejected: Still requires manual buffer management and arbitrary size limits[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Doesn't fix offset calculation bug[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Less maintainable than using standard API[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Alternative [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Change length field to uint8_t**[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Rejected: May break protocol compatibility if some AIM message types actually use[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m-byte lengths[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Doesn't address the fundamental issue of unsafe manual memory operations[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Alternative [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Use dissect_aim_buddyname instead**[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Rejected: Has different interface [0m[1;39m([0m[39mrequires proto_tree, different return [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msemantics[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Would require extensive refactoring of callers[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Uses uint8_t length which may not match all protocol contexts[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
